general 2021-09-04 05:38:45 if so, you'd want to link it to the player.PlayerAdded event
general 2021-09-04 05:42:02 ```
local mps = game:GetService("MarketPlaceService")
local detonator = game.ServerStorage.Detonator -- assuming its a tool
local gamepassid = 000000

game.Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(player) -- fires when player is added
    if mps:UserOwnsGamePassAsync(player.UserId,gamepassid) then --checks if player owns gamepass
      local detonatorclone = detonator:Clone() --clones detonator
      detonatorclone.Parent = player.StarterGear --player will automatically spawn with it
    end
end)
```
